2a1(rgyud): A maN+Dan/ nul

2a3(rgyud): 'jam dpal gyi rtse ba'i rgyud/ sangs

2b2(rgyud): 'di skad bag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das gnas
2b3(rgyud): gtsang ma'i steng gi na mkha'i dkyil na/ byang chub sems dpa' 'dus pa
2b4(rgyud): 'khor gyi tshogs so so tha dad pa bas gyis mi khyab pa'i ngo mtshar rmad du byung
3a1(rgyud): bya/ ba so sor rab tu gnas pa dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs
3a2(rgyud): te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis gnas gtsang ma'i rigs kyi lha'i bu rnams la
3a3(rgyud): bka' stsal pa/ lha'i bu dag khyed cag nyon gcig/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa
3a4(rgyud): chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ ngo mtshar rmad
3b1(rgyud): du byung ba/ ting nge 'dzin bye brag dang / rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par thar pa'i dkyil 'khor byang chub
3b2(rgyud): sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi nye bar 'tsho ba/ tshe dang /
3b3(rgyud): nad med pa dang / dbang phyug dang / yid la bsams pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i sngags kyi
3b4(rgyud): gzhi dag sems can rnams la phan pa'i phyir bshad par byas te/ de shin tu legs par nyon la
3b5(rgyud): yid la zung shig dang / ngas bshad par bya'o// de nas gnas gtsang mo'i rigs kyi lha'i bu de
4a1(rgyud): dag gis thal mo sbyar ba btad nas/ bcom ldan 'das la legs so zhes gso
4a2(rgyud): te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par dang / sa chen po thob par bya ba dang /
4a3(rgyud): rdo rje'i gdan gnon pa dang / bdud 'dul ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / nyan thos dang / rang
4a4(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi nges par 'byung ba dang / lha rnams dang / mi rnams su bskyed par bya ba dang /
4a5(rgyud): sdug bsngal dang / dbul ba dang / nad thams cad zhi bar byed pa/ longs spyod kyis phyag po/ 'dren par
4b1(rgyud): byed pa/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i sngags kyi spyod pas 'phongs par byed mi byed pa/ re ba thams cad yongasu rdzogs
4b2(rgyud): par byed pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsung 'bras bu med par byed pa ma yin pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis byams pa'i
4b3(rgyud): thugs dang / phan pa'i thugs dang / bdag dang sems can thams cad la thugs brtse ba nye bar bzung nas de bshad du gsol/
4b4(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das sha kya thub pas thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor gnas gtsang ma'i gnas la sangs rgyas kyi sman gyis rnam
4b5(rgyud): par gzigs nas dag pa'i yul la rnam par spros te/ yul rnam par 'jig pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs so//
4b6(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das snyoms par bzhugs ma thag tu mdzod spu nas me tog kun tu skyes pa zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' yang dag
5a1(rgyud): bya/ par bskul ba zhes bya ba'i 'od phyung ste/ 'od bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma'i 'khor gyis bcom ldan 'das
5a2(rgyud): lo ldan gsum bskor ba byas nas/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su song nas byang shar gyis phyog su brgya stong gi gang
5a3(rgyud): ga'i klung gi 'jig rten gyis khams 'das nas/ me tog dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rjes su zhugs te/ gang na me tog/
5a4(rgyud): kun tu skyes pa'i rgyal po'i dbang po zhes bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs paro// der yang 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa sngon gyi smon
5a5(rgyud): lom gyis dbang gis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i spyod pa dang ldan pa rnams dang lhan cig gnas par gyur to// 'jim
5a6(rgyud): dpal gzhon nur gyur pas 'od zer gyi snang ba de mthong nas/ bzhin cung zad 'dzum pa dang ldan par gyur nas byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs
5b1(rgyud): de dag la smras pa/ rgyal ba'i sras dag 'od 'di ni nga la yang dag par bskal ba'i phyir 'ongs pa yin gyis/ khyed cag g.yeng ba med par gyis ces smras so//
5b2(rgyud): de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa mig mi 'dzums zhing kha bye bas/ 'od gang na ba de logs mngon du bltas
5b3(rgyud): nas 'dug go/ de nas bskul ba'i 'od des me tog dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyis khams snang ba chen pos snang bar byas te/ me tog kun du
5b4(rgyud): skyes pa zhes bya ba'i rgyal po'i dbang po de bzhin gshegs pa la lan gsum bskor ba byas te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon
5b5(rgyud): nor gyur pa'i spyi bor nub par gyur to// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa bstan las langs te/ bcom ldan 'das me tog kan du yang dag par skyes pa'i
5b6(rgyud): rgyal po'i dbang po de bzhin gshegs pa la lan gsum bskor ba byas te/ spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/
5b7(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das me tog kun du skyes pa'i rgyal po'i dbang po la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba/ de bzhin gshegs
6a1(rgyud): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis bdag la dgongs te/ bcom ldan 'das bdag ni bcom ldan 'das
6a2(rgyud): shAkya thub pa la blta ba dang / phyag bya ba dang / bstan bkar bya ba dang / sngags thams cad kyis spyod pa dang / dkyil 'khor bsgrub thabs dang / dkyil 'khor
6a3(rgyud): dang cho ga dang / gsang ba dang / cho ga zhib mo dang / cho ga'i ngo bo dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs dang / gsang ba dang / phyag rgya dang /
6a4(rgyud): dbang bskur ba bstan pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi kham su 'di nas
6a5(rgyud): 'chi bar 'tshal lo// de skad ces bcom ldan 'das me tog kun tu skyes pa'i rgyal po'i dbang po de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol pa dang / 'jam dpal gzhon
6a6(rgyud): nur gyur pa ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ phyogs bzhi mtha' yas mu med pa'i steng dang / 'og dang / zathad ka thams cad dang ldan pa'i phyogs
6a7(rgyud): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yang dag par gang bar gyur to// 'jig rten gyi khams de'i bcom ldan 'das dang bcas pas rgyal ba'i sras pa
6b1(rgyud): legs so legs so// 'di lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par la snyoms par bzhugs pa ni/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang mi nus/ byang chub
6b2(rgyud): sems dpa' dang / spyod pa la zhugs pa dang / sa bcu la gnas pa dag gis kyang snyoms par zhugs par mi nus so// de nas bcom ldan 'das me tog kun tu yang
6b3(rgyud): dag par skyes pa'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de rnams dang lhan gcig tu yang dag par 'grogs te/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur
6b4(rgyud): gyur pa 'di'i snying po mchog tu bsang ba/ don thams cad sgrub pa'i snying po gsungs pa ni/ yi ge gcig pa zhes bya ba'i mchog tu gsang ba/ sems can thams
6b5(rgyud): cad kyi las thams cad byed pa/ sngags kyi spyod pa khyad par can bzang po yang sgrub par byed pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das me tog yang dag par skyes pa'i rgyal po/
6b6(rgyud): dbang po// de bzhin gshegs pa yud tsamo zhig cang mi gsung bar gyur te/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi skyon gyis gzigs
6b7(rgyud): te sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la yang dag par dgongs nas/ byams pa'i thugs kyis sngags gsungs so// na ma sarba bud+d+hA na ma/ oM mo//
6b8(rgyud): 'di ni 'jam dpal gyi snying po mchog yin te/ las thams cad byed pa'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas/ dper na skyes bu
7a1(rgyud): / stobs dang ldan pa lag pa skum pa las brkyang ba 'am/ se gol togs pa tsam 'am/ mig 'byed 'dzums tsam la rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs/
7a2(rgyud): kyi shugs blo ting nge 'dzin ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyis khyad par 'phrul pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par zhugs te/ mi mdzod kyi 'jig rten gyi khams su chas te song
7a3(rgyud): ba dang / steng gi na mkha'i dkyil na nor bu rin po che rab tu gnas pa'i gnas gtsang ma'i rigs kyi lha rnams su chas te/ gnas gtsang ma'i gnas de thams cad 'od chen po'i
7a4(rgyud): snang bas gsal bar byas te/ 'od rin po ches rab tu brgyan cing gsal ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// rin po che rnam pa tha dad pa du ma'i khang
7a5(rgyud): pa brtsegs pa dang / rin po che'i gdugs dang / dpag tshad brgya stong khrag du ma'i rgyu che ba'i gos dang / dar mang po'i tshogs kyis nye bar mdzes par byas pa'i 'a
7a6(rgyud): dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa de'i dus la bab par shes na song shig/ 'on kyang nga'i bkas bcom
7a7(rgyud): ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la gnod pa nyung ngam/ nyamed pa nyung ngam/ spyod pa yang ngam/ bde ba la rig par gnas sam zhes zhus par bya'o// de nas bcom ldan
7a8(rgyud): 'das me tos yang dag par skyes pa rgyal po'i dbang po de bzhin gshegs pas/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la 'di gad ces bka' stsal to// gzhan mo
7a9(rgyud): rgya 'jam dpal gzhonur gyur pa snyom par zhugs ma thag tu/
7b1(rgyud): gzhon nu gang ga'i klung gi brgya stong gi bye ma snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis khyod kyi sngags kyi spyod pa dang /
7b2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dang / cho ga zhib mo dang / gsang ba dang / dbang bskur ba dang / phyag rgya'i tshogs dang / cho ga dang / sprin bsreg dang / bzlas pa dang /
7b3(rgyud): brtul zhugs bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa/ sems can thams cad dga' bar byed pa/ 'od rin po che rab 'byams 'das pa dang / da ltar byung
7b4(rgyud): ba dang / ma 'ongs par shes pa/ rgyal po'i dbang phyug lung ston par byed pa/ sngags zla ba yul gyi mthar 'gro bar byed pa/ mi snang bar byed pa dang / dus
7b5(rgyud): dang dam tshig rab 'byams kyi tshogs thams cad dang / 'jig rten pa ma lus pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dang /
7b6(rgyud): 'phags pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi nges par 'byung ba'i spyod pa thar thug pa gsungs pa dang / gsung ba dang / gsung bar 'gyur ba yin te/ de ltar rjes
7b7(rgyud): yi rang ba nyid de/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa de'i dus la bab par shes nas song shig/ shAkya thub pa'i spyan sngar mngon sum du chos kyi rnam grangs 'di
7b8(rgyud): thos par 'gyur ro// khyod kyang ston par 'gyur ro// 'dir yang gsungs pa na/ namaHsarba ta thAg ta naM/ a tsim+b+ha sa pra ti ta sha sa~M naM/ oM sarba ra sa pra ti
8a1(rgyud): ha ta sha san/ ku mA ra rU pa ha ri na/ oM hUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA/ 'di ni 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i rtsa ba'i sngags so// de bzhin
8a2(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying pos te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa la/ gsung bar 'gyur la/ khyod kyang mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams su song nas/
8a3(rgyud): dbye ba dang / rnam par dbye ba brgya cher ston par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa zhes bya bas kyang las thams cad byed par rjes su gnang bar 'gyur ro//
8a4(rgyud): 'dir snying po'i mchog tu 'gyur ba ni/ oM wa kye de nam/ 'dir nye ba'i snying po ni/ wa kye hUM/ de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa bcom ldan 'das me tog yang
8a5(rgyud): dag par skyes pa rgyal po'i dbang po de bzhin gshegs pa gnang nas/ bkod pa thams cad kyi rgyan byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang rgyud 'thun pa byang chub kyi snying po zan
8a6(rgyud): pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir/ lha'i me tog rnam par bkod pa dang /
8a7(rgyud): rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / phreng ba'i tshogs dang / rin po che'i dril bu'i dra bas 'brel ba snyan pa'i sgra sgegs pa'i phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i
8b1(rgyud): sa thob par byed pa/ lha'i dri dang / byug pa dang / phreng ba dang / phye ma'i char 'bab par mngon par sprul to// de nas gnas gtsang ma'i rigs kyi lha'i bu
8b2(rgyud): rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i cho 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa mthong nas/ ba spu ldang zhing gnas g.yo ba mthong nas snying 'dar
8b3(rgyud): zhing dngang ste/ ci bdag cag gi 'byor pa nyam par ma gyur tam/ zhes phan tshun du rings par 'gro zhing skad mthon po'i smra ba rtsom par byed de/ 'di skad du bcom
8b4(rgyud): ldan 'das yongs su skyab tu gsol/ shakya thub pa yongs su skyab tu gsol to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis thams cad dang ldan pa'i gnas gtsang ma'i
8b5(rgyud): 'khor rnams la bka' stsal pa/ grogs po dag ma 'jigs shig/ ma 'jigs shig/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon
8b6(rgyud): nur gyur pa 'di ni me tog yang dag par skyes pa'i rgyal po de bzhin gshegs pa de'i spyan snga nas nga la blta ba dang / phyag bya ba dang / bsnyen bkur ba dang /
8b7(rgyud): don chen po'i spyod pa dang / sngags kyi tshig dang / rgya che zhing rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi chog ston pa'i phyir 'ongs pa yin no// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur
9a1(rgyud): pas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa lan gsum bskor ba byas nas/ mig mi 'dzum par bcom ldan 'das la
9a2(rgyud): blta zhing zhabs gnyis la btad de tshig 'bru 'di dag gis bcom ldan 'das la bstod pa// skyes bu bskyed pa khyod phyag 'tshal// skyes mchog khyod la
9a3(rgyud): phyag 'tshal lo// skyes bu gtso bo khyod phyag 'tshal// spyod pa thams cad don sgrub pa/ skyes bu seng ge khyod phyag 'tshal// phung khrol thams
9a4(rgyud): cad bzlog byed pa// dpa' bo chen po khyod phyag 'tshal// ngan 'gro thams cad 'jig byed pa/ skyes bu pad dkar khyod phyag 'tshal/
9a5(rgyud): kun nas bsod nams dri ldan pa// skyes bu pad+ma khyod phyag 'tshal// srid gsum 'dam ni rnam dag byed// rnam grol khyod la phyag 'tshal lo//
9a6(rgyud): sdug bsngal ma lus rnam grol byed/ zhing 'gyur khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// thams cad mkhyen pa legs 'dul byed// thams cad grub
9a7(rgyud): pa khyod phyag 'tshal// sngags kyi spyod pa don grub byed// ba kra shis khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// bkra shis kun gyi bkra shis pa// sangs rgyas kun
9b1(rgyud): la khyod phyag 'tshal// chos kun rnam par rtogs mdzad pa// chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid spros pa med pa'i ngo bo yang dag par rjes su zhugs zhing ston par
9b2(rgyud): byed pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa khyed la phyag 'tshal lo// shes pa dang / shes bya'i dngos po thams cad dang / 'dus byas dang / 'dus ma byas dang /
9b3(rgyud): theg pa gsum gyi lam dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i lam la 'jog par byed pa dang / gnas par byed pa thams cad mkhyen pa khyod la phyag 'tshal lo//
9b4(rgyud): zhes tshig 'bra 'di dag gi gsang ba'i bstod pa'i tshig gis bcom ldan 'das la mngon sum du bstod nas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das
9b5(rgyud): 'di gang ga'i klung brgya phrag stong gi bye ma snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams nas byang shar gyi phyogs 'tshams na me tog yang dag par skyed pa zhes bya ba'i sangs
9b6(rgyud): rgyas kyi zhing mchis te/ de na me tog dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams na gang du bcom ldan 'das me tog yang dag par skyes pa dbang po'i rgyal
9b7(rgyud): bo de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabasu ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes
10a1(rgyud): bu 'dul ba/ kha lo bsgyur ba lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa de chos ston to// thog mar dge ba/ bar du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba/ don
10a2(rgyud): bzang po// tshig 'bru bzang po// ma 'dres pa/ yong su rdzog pa/ yongs su dag pa/ yongs su dkar ba/ tshangs par spyod pa yang dag par ston to//
10a3(rgyud): de da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing bzhes la chos ston to// sngags kyi spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod dang / lam gsum gyi spyod pa'i lam sgrub par byed
10a4(rgyud): pa/ skyob pa dang / gnas dang / skyabs dang / dpung gnyen dang / bde ba dang / shin tu mthar thug pa dang / shin tu yongasu mthar phyin par byed pa sems
10a5(rgyud): can rnams la ston te/ bcom ldan 'das de nyid kyi rjes gnang nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs drung 'dir mchis so// de nyid bcom ldan 'das me tog yang
10a6(rgyud): dag par skyes pa rgyal po'i dbang po de yang bcom ldan 'das la gnod pa nyung ngam/ spyod pa yang ngam/ bde ba la reg par gnas sam/ zhes 'dri'o// 'di skad
10a7(rgyud): kyang gsungs te/ gang du 'di lta bu'i snyigs ma lnga'i dus su sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa 'byung ba ni ngo mtshar che'o zhes zer ro// de yang lam gsum
10b1(rgyud): dang / byang sgrol dang / mir skye ba nyid thob pa nyid kyi chos ston par byed do// gang du yang sems can gyi ris skal pa med pa dang / srid pa gsum yang dag par
10b2(rgyud): 'joms par byed pa'i lam dang / gtan du grub pa dang / bde ba 'thun pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa la sems can rnams bkod par byed pa'i bcom ldan 'das
10b3(rgyud): shAkya thub pa'i brtson 'grus ni ngo mtshar to// bcom ldan 'das bsams kyis mi khyab bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs ni sangs rgyas bcom
10b4(rgyud): ldan 'das kyi mkhyen par gyur gyis/ bdag gi ci zhig 'tshal ba rngo thog/ dbang phyug gi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab/ rmad du byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan
10b5(rgyud): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas rnams kyi rnam par 'phrul pa shes par 'am/ 'tshal bar ram/ thugs kyi spyad pa spyod pa'i rjes 'jug pa'i sgrub pa dang / spyod pa 'tshal
10b6(rgyud): bar ram/ mdor na bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi bar du yang bstan par mi nus so// gang yang de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i
10b7(rgyud): mdzad pa bsdus pa 'am/ tha dad pa ma lus pa'i ngo bo 'di ni chos 'dus ma byas su lta bar byas te/ mthong bas spang bar bya ba la rten pa 'am/
11a1(rgyud): @yon tan ni bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa kho nas mkhyen pa yin gyi/ bdag gis ni ma lags so// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas
11a2(rgyud): rang gi rdzu 'phral gyi rnam par 'phrul pas rin po che'i pad ma'i sprul pa la com ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la blta zhing 'dug go// de nas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pas byang chub sems
11a3(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang rjes su 'thun pa'i gtam rnam pa sna tshogs sngon du 'gro ba mdzad nas chos ston pa dang rjes
11a4(rgyud): su 'thun pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa sgrub pa dang rjes su 'thun pas/ tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang / ka la ping ka'i skad dang / 'brug sgra dang / rnga bo che'i sgra skad kyi
11a5(rgyud): gsung gi dbyangs kyis 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa khyod legs par 'ongs sam/ sems dpa' chen po'i spyod pa
11a6(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs pa sgrub pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi don thob par byed pa/ sngags thams cad kyi tshig dang / gsang ba dang / bcas
11a7(rgyud): pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / phyag rgya dang / dkyil 'khor dang / cho ga dang / tshe dang / nad med pa dang / dbang phyug dang / bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed
11a8(rgyud): pa/ sgrub pa'i thabs thams cad dang ldan pa/ rgyud shes pa/ shes bya dang / dus dang / mi snang ba dang / rgyal po'i zhing du gyur pa/ 'das pa/ ma 'ongs pa/ da ltar byung ba shes
11b1(rgyud): thams cad byed pa ste/ yid la re ba
11b2(rgyud): par byed pa/ mdor na sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa/ rang gi yon tan dang rjes su 'thun pa'i sngags kyi spyod pa rjes su 'jug pa/ sems
11b3(rgyud): can gzhan dga' bar byed pa/ mi snang bar nam mkha' la 'gro ga chu la mi nub par 'gro ba/ yid bzhangs par byed pa/ 'gags par byed pa/ sa 'og tu 'jug pa/ mngon du
11b4(rgyud): spyod par byed pa/ 'dod pa thams cad thob par byed pa/ gnod sbyin dang / gnod sbyin mo dang / mngag gzhag pa dang / sha za dang / 'byung po thams cad 'gags par byed pa/
11b5(rgyud): byis pa dang / rgan po dang / gzhon nu gnas ji lta ba bzhin du 'jog par byed pa/ mdor na las thams cad rdzogs par byed pa/ mngon spyod dang / rgyas pa dang / zhi ba'i las dag
11b6(rgyud): rab tu byed pa ji lta ji ltar rab tu sbyor ba de lta de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod phal po che/ bskal pa chen po'i rin po che'i le'u rab 'byam 'di ngas kyang rjes su gnang zhing /
11b7(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi kyang gsungs te/ sems can dag rang gi sngags spyod pa'i don gyi chos kyi mdzod skye bo mang po la phan pa dang / skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / lha dang / mi rnam
11b8(rgyud): dang sems can thams cad kyi don du bstan pa'i phyir ro// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyi brlabs pa'i 'od kyi snang ba bkod pa'i brgyan
11b9(rgyud): yang dag par bskal pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ dag pa'i sems can gyi 'od kyi snang bas gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed du mi
12a1(rgyud): mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'og min gyi gnas kyi bar dang / mnar med pa'i dmyal ba chen po'i bar du khyab par byas te/
12a2(rgyud): sems can gang su dag shin tu sdug bsngal ba de dag thams cad kyi sdug bsngal rab tu zhi bar gyur to// nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / sangs rgyas bcom
12a3(rgyud): ldan 'das rnams yang dag par skal nas/ 'od de 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i spyi bo'i brtsag tu nub par gyur to// 'dir gang dag shar phyogs nas rnam par gnas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing
12a4(rgyud): der 'od zer rlung gi dkyil 'khor gyi reg pa'i bya bas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das yang dag par bskal te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis zla ba dri snang ba'i dpal zhes bya ba dang /
12a5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa sman bla bai DUr+ya'i 'od dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dpal kan du snang ba zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dag par 'phags pa zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin/
12a6(rgyud): gshegs pa sa la'i dbang po'i rgyal po zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi dbang po'i rgyal po zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa'i ye shes
12a7(rgyud): rnam par nges pa'i rgyal po zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa snang ba mtha' yas dbang po'i rgyal po zhes bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa snang ba'i 'od kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba dang /
12a8(rgyud): de dag la sogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis yongs su bskor ba/ mtha' yas mu med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams dag nas de bzhin gshegs pa
12b1(rgyud): dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dag la/ mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi gnas gtsang ma'i khang bzangs na de bzhin gshegs pa
12b2(rgyud): dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa dang / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa lhan tu byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa ston pa dang / sngags kyi tshig gi don gyi le'u
12b3(rgyud): rab 'byam ston to// de bzhin du lho dang / nub dang / byang gi phyogs dang / phyogs 'tshams dang / steng dang / 'og dang / thang dkar thams cad dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing
12b4(rgyud): snang bar byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du bdud kyi gnas thams cad pa skong bar byas nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs thams cad kyi yongs su bskor cing / nyan thos
12b5(rgyud): kyi dge 'dun dang bcas pas mdun gyis bltas te/ gnas gtsang ma'i gnas su sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bdag nyid chen po blta bar 'dod pa dang / sngags
12b6(rgyud): kyi spyod pa sgrub pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi khyad par dang / le'u tshogs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa thogs pa med pa gsal bar 'dod pas chags pa ni/ 'di lta ste/
12b7(rgyud): lag bzang dang / rin chen bzang po dang / brtul zhugs bzang po dang / spyan mdzes dang / bzang dga' dang / chos bzang dang / don thams cad grub pa dang / thams cad du 'phags
12b8(rgyud): ba dang chos 'phags pa dang / rin chen 'phags dang / rin chen dpal dang / lhun po'i dpal dang / bsam gyi mi khyab pa'i dpal dang / 'od byed dpal dang / 'od dpal dang /
13a1(rgyud): @#/ don thams cad kyi dpal dang / thams cad phyag na rin po dang / phyag na btsug gi rin po che dang / phyag na lhun po'i rgyal po dang / rnam par snang mdzad snying po
13a2(rgyud): dang / rin chen snying po dang / ye shes snying po dang / bsam gyi mi khyab pa don gyi snying po dang / chos 'phags kyi snying po dang / rgyal mtshan gyi tog dang / tog bzangs dang /
13a3(rgyud): mtha' yas tog dang / dri ma med pa'i tog dang / mtha' dag gi tog dang / na mkha'i tog dang / rin po che'i tog dang / 'brug sgra dang / rnga bo che'i skad kyi rgyal po dang /
13a4(rgyud): mtha' yas par snang ba'i ye shes kyi rgyal po dang / mun pa mun nag thams cad 'joms pa'i rgyal po dang / gnod pa thams cad rnam par 'jig pa'i rgyal po dang / spyod pa
13a5(rgyud): thams cad kyi yul shes pa'i rgyal po dang / 'jig rten gyi dbang po'i rgyal po dang / mngon par rtogs pa'i dbang po'i rgyal po dang / rnam par 'joms par byed pa'i rgyal po dang /
13a6(rgyud): nges par g.yo bar byed pa'i rgyal po dang / nyi ma'i rgyal po dang / dngos po med par yang dag par 'phags pa'i rgyal po dang / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid yang dag par 'phags
13a7(rgyud): ba'i rgyal po dang / mi 'thun pa'i phyogs med pa'i rgyal po dang / rang bzhin gyi 'od dang / bsod nams 'od dang / 'jig rten 'od dang / dpag med 'od dang / mtha' yas
13a8(rgyud): 'od dang / spyan bzang 'od dang / 'byung med 'od dang / don gyi 'od dang / mi tshugs pa dang / bzod dka' ba dang / las med dang / 'od min dang / dri med dang /
13b1(rgyud): me dang / 'od dang / blo dang / rtogs pa dang / bde ba'i mu khyud dang / mu khyud rtog dang / 'dod pa'i lha dang / lha dang lha yul na yod pa dang / lte ba dang / rgya ba dang /
13b2(rgyud): 'jig rten zhi ba dang / nye bar 'dod pa dang / rnga bo che dang / grub pa dang / dkar po dang / grags bzangs dang / bzod par bka' ba dang / gdul bka' ba dang /
13b3(rgyud): rnyed par dka' ba dang / ring du song ba dang / ring ba'i don dang / ring ba la gnas pa dang / mtho ba dang / shin tu mtho ba dang / srin bu me khyer dang / kun tu snang ba dang /
13b4(rgyud): snang med dang / khyu mchog dang / kun nas 'od dang / shin tu yid du 'ong ba dang / yid bzangs dang / lha chen po dang / dri med bzang po dang / dri ma mthar byed dang /
13b5(rgyud): dul ba dang / zhing ldan dang / mtshan bzang dang / rgyal mtshan dkar po dang / tshad ldan dang / ci smra dang / tha chung dang / sel byed dang / 'tsho ba dang / legs skyes
13b6(rgyud): dang / dad pa'i rtog dang / rgyal mtshan tog dang / dkar ba'i tog dang / rtog bzang dang / nor lha'i tog dang / nor lha'i bu dang / mes po dang / pha dang / mthar byed dang /
13b7(rgyud): 'jig rten grags pa dang / kun nas grags pa dang / grags pa chen po dang / dpal ldan dang / pham byed dang / 'od byed dang / mngag gzhug pa dang / zhi byed dang /
13b8(rgyud): 'jig rten byed dang / lha byed dang / mtho rigs byed dang / mar me mdzad dang / 'byung po mthar byed dang / don thams cad mdzad dang / grub mdzad dang / gsal
14a1(rgyud): mdzad dang / snang bar mdzad pa dang / rnga bo che'i sgra dang / skad kyi sgra dang / sgra bstan dang / mtha' yas pa'i sgra dang / rtog gi sgra dang / ngan spong gi
14a2(rgyud): bu dang / gser thub dang / 'khor ba 'jig dang / 'od srungs dang / gtsug gtor can dang / thams cad skyob dang / rnam par gzigs dang / shakya thub pa dang / gzhan
14a3(rgyud): yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mang po dag gis gnas gtsang ma'i gzhal med khang snang bar byas te/ pad ma'i gdan la bzhugs par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa'i chog
14a4(rgyud): kyang de lta bu'i tshul du lhags par gyur to// 'di lta ste/ phyag na rin chen dang / phyag na rdo rje dang / mnyam pa'i phyag dang / na mkha'i phyag dang / mtha' yas phyag dang /
14a5(rgyud): sa'i phyag dang / snang ba'i phyag dang / dri med bzang po dang / bzang brtsegs dang / rab mang brtsegs dang / nor bu brtsegs dang / rin chen brtsegs dang / rin chen
14a6(rgyud): phyag dang / kun nas phyag dang / dri ldan phyag dang / legs 'gro dang / dri med 'gro dang / 'jig rten 'gros dang / mdzes pa'i 'gros dang / mtha' yas 'gros dang /
14a7(rgyud): grags pa mtha' yas dang / grags pa bzang po dang / grags pa dri ma bral ba dang / grags pa'i 'gro ba dang / grags pa dri ma med pa dang / grags pa dang / grags pa 'dren
14a8(rgyud): pa dang / mgon po dang / mgon por gyur pa dang / kun nas mgon po dang / rgyun shes kyi bu dang / mtha' yas rgyun shes kyi bu dang / kun nas rgyun shes kyi bu dang / byams pa'i
14b1(rgyud): bu dang / byams pa bzang po'i bu dang / byams pa'i bu ma yin pa dang / dus gsum rgyun shes dang / rgyun shes kyi 'bras bu dang bcas pa dang / rgyun shes kyi bu dkon mchog
14b2(rgyud): gsum dang / rgyun shes kyi bu skyabs gsum dang / rgyun shes kyi bu theg gsum dang / rnam par sprul pa dang ldan pa dang / yid 'ong bzang po dang / gsung snyan ldan dang /
14b3(rgyud): chos kyi dbang phyug dang / dngos med dbang phyug dang / 'jig rten dbang phyug dang / spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dang / legs gzigs dbang phyug dang / rnam gzigs dbang phyug dang /
14b4(rgyud): 'jig rten chos 'os dang / legs mchod dang / sgra sgrogs dbang phyug dang / rnga chen dbang phyug dang / sna tshogs sgra'i dbang phyug dang / rnam 'jig dbang phyug dang / mthong dka' bzang
14b5(rgyud): skra mdzes dang / lha grags ldan dang / nyi ma'i 'od dang / khyab 'jug bdag po dang / bdag po'i ngang tshul dang / na mkha'i snying po dang / don thams cad kyi snying po dang / thams cad
14b6(rgyud): 'byung ba dang / ngan song spong ba dang / phyir mi ldog pa dang / chos ma yin pa gcod par byed pa dang / de dag dang / gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams dang
14b7(rgyud): lhan cig tu/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa gnas gtsang ma'i gzhal med khang na bzhugs so// gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bud med kyi gzugs 'chang ba
14b8(rgyud): rnams te/ spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i don 'jig rten bsgrub pa'i don/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa phyir mi ldog pa'i lam la dgod pas bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i tshig dang /
15a1(rgyud): sngags kyi tshig dang / gzungs dang / sman gyi cha byad 'dzin pa dang / 'dab chags kyi tshogs rnam pa sna tshogs dang / gnod sbyin dang / srin po dang /
15a2(rgyud): nor bu dang / sngags dang / rin po che'i rgyal po dang / sems can thams cad kyi lus kyi grangs su rjes su yang dag par 'jug pa'i spyod pa thams cad kyi rjes su 'jug pa dang /
15a3(rgyud): sems can gyi bsam pa ji ltar 'dul bar byed pa'i de bzhin du byed pa rnams dang / de dag rjes su 'thun pa'i ming dang / 'brel ba dang / rig pa'i rgyal po nye bar brtan pa dang /
15a4(rgyud): chos ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs pa las nges par 'byung ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dang / pad+ma dang / rdo rje'i rigs dang / 'jig rten dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rig
15a5(rgyud): kyi rjes su zhugs pa/ dam tshig las mi 'da' zhing / tshig gi lam la 'jog par byed pa/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rgyun mi gcod par byed pa yin te/ 'di lta ste/
15a6(rgyud): gtsug gtor dang / mngon par 'phags pa dang / mngon par mtho ba dang / bdugs dkar po dang / 'dab ma mtha' yas dang / 'dab ma brgya pa dang / rgyal ba'i gtsug gtor
15a7(rgyud): dang / 'jig rten mthon po dang / rnam par rgyal ba'i btsug gtor dang / mngon par 'phags pa'i btsug gtor dang / pad+ma'i 'od dang / me tog pad ma'i 'od dang / me tog ka ta
15a8(rgyud): ka'i 'od dang / 'od dkar po dang / bkod pa'i gtsug gtor dang / gser gyi phung po dang / dkar po'i phung po dang / gzi brjid phung po dang / nor bu'i phung po dang / kun nas
15b1(rgyud): phung po dang / rnam par grags pa'i phung po dang / 'byung ba'i phung po dang / bden pa'i phung po dang / dngos po med pa'i ngo bo'i phung po dang / de kho na nyid kyi phung po dang / de dag dang /
15b2(rgyud): gzhan yang gtsug gtor gyi rgyal po chos kyi dbyings mtha' yas pa la rab tu zhugs pa/ sems can gyi bsam pa rab tu rdzogs par byed pa/ rgyal ba thams cad kyi snying po
15b3(rgyud): dang ldan pa gtsug gtor gyi rgyal po bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi bar du yang bgrang zhing mthar thug par mi nus so// stobs dang pha rol gnon pa bsam gyis mi khyab
15b4(rgyud): pa'i bdag nyid kyang bstan par mi nus so// mdor bstan par bya ste/ brjod pa ni rig pa'i rgyal mo'i 'das pa brjod par bya ste/ 'di lta ste/ mdzod spu dang / smin ma dang / spyan
15b5(rgyud): dang / rdzi ma dang / rna ba dang / mgrin pa dang / mi 'jigs pa dang / snying rje dang / byams pa dang / brtse ba dang / shes rab dang / 'od zer dang / sems dpa' dang / 'od dang /

15b7(rgyud): dag ni/ 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i snod dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzims mal dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i snang
15b8(rgyud): ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhal dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i brla dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / de bzhin gshegs

16a2(rgyud): po dang / rgyal mo dang / mngag gzhug pa dang / bran po dang / bran mo dang / pho nya dang / pho nya mo dang / gnod sbyin dang / gnod sbyin mo dang / sems can dang / sems can/

17a7(rgyud): grub pa mtha' yas pas chos kyi dbyings na mkha' dang 'dra ba'i ngo bo dang / sems can gyi spyod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa la gnas pa las byung ba'i yid dang / pho nya dang /
17a8(rgyud): pho nya mo dang / bran po dang / bran mo dang / mngag gzhug pa dang / mngag gzhug ma dang / gnod sbyin dang / gnod sbyin mo dang / srin po dang / srin mo dang / sha za dang /
17b1(rgyud): sha za mo dang / pad ma'i rigs dam tshig la rjes su zhugs shing rjesu spyod pa rnams dang / gnas gtsang ma'i lha'i gzhal med khang sems can dag pa gang na 'dug pa der phyin
17b2(rgyud): par gyur to// byin nas kyang bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la mchod pa'i las la sogs pa'i yid kyi der gnas par gyur to/ der gnas pa na bcom ldan 'das shAkya

23b7(rgyud): ka bud+d+ha A ru shra ba ka nam/ na ma bo d+hi satwA nam/ da sha b+hU mi pra tiSh+Thi te shwa di nam/ bo d+hi satwA nam/ ma hA sad+hA nam/ tad+ya thA/ oM kha kha kha hi khA hi duSh+Ta sa sang+ga ma/ kra a sa
23b8(rgyud): mu sa la ba ra shu pA dwe sha hAs+t+ra/ tsa tud b+hu dza/ tsa tur mu khI/ ShaT tsa ran/ gang+ga gang+gA/ sarba big+h+na/ bib+ha ta ke bi kri ta nan/ sarba bud+d+ha pa yang+kar/ at+pa twAM ha sa/ ni na di na/
24a1(rgyud): b+hag+h+nAn+ta ma/ nimaH/ rmAk+Shan+tu/ sarba rmAms/ smye / sam/ hrI we/ ba gyur// gnas sa gnas/ sarba g+huSh+Ta/

30a1(rgyud): pad ma ltar smra ba dang / 'jigs byed ma dang / mi 'jigs sbyin ma dang / rgyal byed ma dang / rnam par rgyal ma dang / nam phra ma dang /
30a2(rgyud): sgra gcan ma dang / skra mthar byed ma dang / rlung ma dang / yid 'phrog ma dang / yid ldan ma dang / me tog ldan ma dang / me tog gi grong khyer la gnas ma dang / ser kye ma dang / 'phrog mo dang /
30a3(rgyud): dpal ldan ma dang / dpa' mo dang / dpa' bzang mo dang / shin tu mi bzad ma dang / mi bzang ldan ma dang / lha mdzes ma dang / ro langs ma dang / gsang ba dam pa ma dang / shing ma la
30a4(rgyud): gnas ma dang / mya ngan med ma dang / mun par mdzes ma dang / 'od ldan ma dang / lhag par ldan ma dang / gzugs mdzes ma dang / dkar med ma dang / zhi ba ma dang / phyogs
30a5(rgyud): mtshams ma dang / sdug ma dang / dga' byed ma dang / nye ba'i dga' byed ma dang / 'jig rten las 'das ma ste/ gnod srin mo chen po 'di dag kyang gnod srin mo brgya stong phrag du
30a6(rgyud): ma'i 'khor dang ldan pa/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po dar rgyang ring po nyid nas/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la phyag 'tshol zhing ma khod par gyur to// gang yang sha za mo dag sha za
30a7(rgyud): mo rgya stong phrag du ma'i 'khor dang ldan pa 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor der rgyang ring po nyid nas/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa la phyag 'tshal zhing mchod par gyur to// 'di lta ste/ sdud ma dang /
30a8(rgyud): phyag dar khrod kyi sha za mo dang / sha za mi drag mo dang / sha za mo skar mda' dang / sha za mo 'bar ma dang / thal ba za ma dang / sha za dang / dag ma dang / bung ba dang / rmongs byed ma dang /
30b1(rgyud): sdigs 'dzub ma dang / dmar ldan ma dang / glang dmar ma dang / 'jig rten nye gnas ma dang / thal ba nye gnas pa dang / shing bu lu ldan ma dang / mang ldan ma dang / mang ma dang /
30b2(rgyud): gdul dka' ma dang / e la ma dang / me tshon byed ma de/ du la gnas ma dang / du ba ma ste/ sha za mo chen mo 'di dag kyang sha za mo'i 'khor bya ba brgya stong phrag du ma dang bcas pa de dag
30b3(rgyud): kyang 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po der 'dus shing rab tu zhugs par gyur to// gang yang ma me dang / ma mo chen mo dag 'jig rten gyi rjes su rnam par smod cing sems can rnams la 'tshe bar
30b4(rgyud): byed de/ gtor ma dang / me tog dang sman la skrod par byed pa dag la/ 'di lta ste/ tshangs pa ma dang / dbang phyug chen po ma dang / khyab 'jug ma dang / gzhon nu ma dang / rgan byed ma dang /
30b5(rgyud): phag mo dang / dbang mo dang / gshin rje mo dang / me phyogs ma dang / nyi mi'i bu me dang / 'jig rten mthar byed me dang / chu lha ma dang / dbang ldan ma dang / rlung phyogs ma dang /
30b6(rgyud): gzhan gyi srog 'phrog ma dang / mgo bregs ma dang / bya ma dang / bya ma chen mo dang / srul mo dang / lus srul mo dang / skab byed ma ste/ ma mo chen mo de dag ma me'i 'khor bye ba
30b7(rgyud): khri khrag rgya stong du ma dang / bcas pa de dag kyang 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po der sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo zhes pa'i tshig 'don cing 'khod par gyur to// de bzhin du mi dang mi ma yin pa
30b8(rgyud): byeg khri zag 'gyi stong du ma dang / sems canas yin panas dmyal ba chen po mnar med panas/ srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du thams cad kyang skabs 'dir na mkha'i dkyil du
31a1(rgyud): snang bar gyur te/ sems can gyi rigs/ srog chags su la yang mi 'thun pa med par gyur to// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi
31a2(rgyud): brlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i cho 'phrul gyi rgyan gyis/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang / 'jam dpal gzhon nar gyur pa sems can thams cad
31a3(rgyud): kyi spri gtsug na bzhugs pa mthong bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pas thams can dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi sman gyi rnam par
31a4(rgyud): gzibs nas/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la bka' stsal pa/ dge pa'i sems pa sngags kyi spyod pa'i don rnam par gtan la dbab pa dang / ting nge 'dzin
31a5(rgyud): gyi le'u rab 'byams byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod gang 'di bshad pa'i dus la bab par sems pa na shog/ de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa/ bcom ldan
31a6(rgyud): 'das shAkya thub pas rjes su gnang ba mdzad pa na/ nam mkha'i ngo bo dang 'dra ba rdo rje thug cing sra ba'i rgyud bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs te/
31a7(rgyud): 'dzam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa de snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ gnas gtsang ming gzhal med khang de dpag tshad brgya stong du ma/ rgya che ba rdo rje'i rang bzhin du
31a8(rgyud): gnas lhag par gnas par gyur to// gang gnod sprin dang / srin po dang / dri za dang / yi dgas dang / rlung lha dang / sha za de dag dang / mdor
31b1(rgyud): na sems can gyi khams thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis/ gzhal med de dag rdo rje nor bu rin po che lta bur gyur te/ der rab tu zhugs te ma khod par
31b2(rgyud): gyur kyang phan tshun rnam par 'tshe ba byed pa med do// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nor gyur pas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po der 'das par shes nas// khro bo'i rgyal
31b3(rgyud): po gshin rje gshed la smras pa/ kye khro bo chen po sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi rjes su nges par 'byung bar byed pa/ 'khor gyi
31b4(rgyud): dkyil 'khor chen po 'dus pa 'di'i sems can thams cad la srungs shig/ bsrungs shig/ dbang du gyis shig/ mi rung ba 'dul bar gyis shig/
31b5(rgyud): sems can zhi ba dag sad par gyis shig/ sems can thams cad dad par gyis shig/ ji srid du da'i rang bzhin gi sngags kyi skrod pa rjes su bsgrub pa/
31b6(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod rgya che ba dag las sngags pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'chad par byed pa de srid kyi bar du/ 'di dag phyi rol du song ba slongs shig/ de skad
31b7(rgyud): ces smras pa dang / khro bo'i rgyal pos mnyan nas/ khro bo chen po'i gzugs kyi sems can thams cad rjes su bsrung ba dang / rjes su brtan pa'i phyir 'khor gyi
31b8(rgyud): dkyil 'khor thams cad du/ khro bo'i rgyal po gshin rje gshed khro bo'i 'khor brgya stong phrag du ma phyogs bzhi kun dang / steng dang / 'og dang / thad ka dag tu gshin
32a1(rgyud): du mi bzad pa'i sgra rab tu 'don cing 'khod par gyur to// de nas sems can de dag zhi ba dang / yid dang / sems bzang po dang ldan par gyur te/
32a2(rgyud): bka' las mi 'da' bar gyur to// 'di lta bu'i sgra yang rab tu thos par gyur to// gang dam tshig 'di las 'da' bar byed pa de dag ni a rdza ka'i dog pa bzhin du mgo bo tshal
32a3(rgyud): pa brgyar 'gas par 'gyur te/ de ni byang chub sems dpa'i byin gyis brlabs kyang de yin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas/
32a4(rgyud): rang gi sngags kyi smod pa'i don du chos kyi tshig smras pa/ chos gcig la yang dag par bsams na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i sngags grub pa yin te/
32a5(rgyud): gcig po gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad spros pa med pa'i rnam par rjes su mthob pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos gnyis la rab tu gnas
32a6(rgyud): na sngags 'grub par 'gyur te/ gnyis po gang zhe na/ byang chub kyi sems mi gtong ba nyid dang / sems can thams cad la sems mnyam pa'o// chos gsum dang
32a7(rgyud): ldan na sngags kyi spyod pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur te/ gsum po gang zhe na/ sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba nyid dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshul
32a8(rgyud): khrims kyi sdom po bsrung ba dang / rang gi sngags yongs su gtong ba nyid do// chos bzhi dang yang dag par ldan na/ dang po sems bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i
32b1(rgyud): sngags 'grub par 'gyur te/ bzhi po gang zhe na/ rang gi sngags yongs su mi gtong ba nyid dang / gzhan gyi sngags rjes su dpyod pa mang ba nyid dang / sems can thams
32b2(rgyud): cad la byams pas gnas pa nyid dang / snying rje chen po yongs su bsgom pa'i sems dpa' nyid dang / chos bzhi po 'di dag dang ldan na/ dang po sems bskyed pa'i byang chub
32b3(rgyud): sems dpa'i sngags grub par 'gyur ro// chos lnga dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod la 'jug cing / sngags kyi spyod pa bslab pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur te/
32b4(rgyud): lnga gang zhe na/ rnam par dben pa'i phyogs yang dag par brtan pa nyid dang / bas mtha'i dgon pa brtan par byed pa nyid dang / sems can gzhan la zhe sdang med pa
32b5(rgyud): nyid dang / 'jig rten pa'i sngags la mi lta ba nyid dang / tshul khrims dang / thos pa dang / sprod pa la gnas par byed pa nyid de/ chos lnga po 'di dag dang ldan na sngags spyod pa'i
32b6(rgyud): don brab cing / yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// chos drag dang ldan na sngags kyi spyod pa grub ci nga yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur te/ drag po gang zhe na/ dkon mchog gsum po la
32b7(rgyud): dad pa dang rjes su spyod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' la dad pa rjes mi spyod pa nyid dang / 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i sngags la kun tu dga' ba nyid dang / chos
32b8(rgyud): kyi dbyings spros pa med pa la blta ba nyid dang / theg pa chen po'i mdo sde zab pa'i tshig gi don mi spong zhing / skyo ba med pa'i sems nyid dang / sngags kyi spyod pa yongs su btsal ba nyid dang /
33a1(rgyud): / dge ba'i phyogs yongs su mi gtong ba nyid de/ chos drub po 'di dag dang ldan na rig pa'i spyod pa dang ldan zhing sngags grub cing yang dag par sgrub pa nyid du 'gyur ro//
33a2(rgyud): chos bdun dang ldan na/ rig pa bsgrub pa'i dus kyi thabs thob par 'gyur zhing / sngags kyi dpyod pa la rjes su spyod pa nyid du 'gyur te/ bdun po gang zhe na/ theg pa chen po shes rab kyi
33a3(rgyud): pha rol tu phyin pa zam mo nyid bsgom pa dang / klog pa dang / ston pa dang / 'don du 'jug pa dang / 'bri ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la mos pa nyid dang / dus dang /
33a4(rgyud): phyogs dang / nges par sdom pa dang / bzlas pa dang / sprin bsreg dang / mi smra ba dang / dka' thub la gzhol ba nyid dang / rtogs pa dang / blo dang / dran pa dang / shes
33a5(rgyud): rab dang / brtan pa la bsnyen pa nyid dang / byang chub kyi tshogs dang / theg pa chen po dang / zab pa'i chos kyi tshul la yang dag par rab tu zhugs pa nyid dang / rang dga'i
33a6(rgyud): sngags dgug pa'i bya ba la mkhas pa nyid dang / snying rje chen po nyid dang / byams pa chen po dang / btang snyoms chen po dang / dga' ba chen po nyid yongs su bsgom
33a7(rgyud): pa nyid dang / spros pa med pa'i sems can gyi khams kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi de bzhin nyid la 'jug pa gnyis su med pa'i ngo bo'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs
33a8(rgyud): su 'chol pa nyid dang / sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba nyid dang / theg pa dman po la dga' ba med pa nyid de/ chos 'dun po dag gi ni rig pa dang / sngags
33b1(rgyud): grub cing yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// chos brgyad dang ldan na/ rig pa dang sngags kyi spyod pa'i don grub cing lam du 'gro bar 'gyur te/ brgyad po gang zhe na/ mthong
33b2(rgyud): ba dang / mthong ba'i 'bras bu dag pa la blta ba dang / sems par 'dod pa nyid dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par
33b3(rgyud): 'phrul pa nyid la the tshom med cing dang ba nyid dang / phyin ci ma log pa'i sngags bzung ba dang / bla ma la gus pa nyid dang / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' nyid
33b4(rgyud): kyi sngags dang / rgyud dang / spyod pa brtan pa mi klu ba bzang zhing / 'dog pa thams cad yongs su gtong ba nyid dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gnas dang gnas ma yin
33b5(rgyud): pa rmi lam na mthong ba rab tu ston pa la mkhas pa nyid dang / ser sna dang / gnyid dang / rmugs pa mtha' dag dang bral bar byed cing / rtag tu brtson 'grus brtsom
33b6(rgyud): la/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' la bdag nyid dbul bar byed pa nyid dang / mdor brtan dge ba'i rtsa ba chog mi shes shing go cha chen po bgos pa dang /
33b7(rgyud): bgegs thams cad rab tu sel bar 'dod pa nyid dang / byang chub kyi snying po'i 'dod pa dang / longs spyod chen po dang / dbang che bar grags par bdag nyid 'dod
33b8(rgyud): ba dang / dbang che bar grags pa'i gang zag la bsnyen pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang mi 'bral bar bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gzhon
34a1(rgyud): nur gyur pa la nye bar gnas pa nyid de/ chos brgyad po 'di dag dang ldan na/ sngags spyad pa'i don grub pa'i yang dag pa'i lam du 'gyur ro//
34a2(rgyud): grogs po dag mdor na/ byang chub kyi sems dang mi 'bral ba dang / dkon mchog gsum la dad pa dang / mchog tu sdug bsngal zhing tshul khrims nyam pa la yang
34a3(rgyud): mi skyo ba'i yid kyi rtag tu mngon par brtson pa la nga'i sngags kyi le'u rab 'byam mtha' yas shing rmad du byung ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rgyu 'thun pa'i yid
34a4(rgyud): las byung ba 'grub par 'gyur te/ de las gzhan du shes par bya ba ma yin no// rnam par rtog pa med pa'i yid du byas nas/ nyams sad pa'i phyir yang bsgrub par bya/
34a5(rgyud): ba yin no// de nas thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / 'phags pa nyan thos rnams kyis byin gyis
34a6(rgyud): brlabs pa dag gi 'di skad du tshig brjod par bya ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag legs so legs so// sngags spyod pa'i don rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i bya ba chos kyi tshul la rjes su 'jug
34a7(rgyud): pa dang 'thun zhing chos bstan pa legs par bstan pa ni sems can thams cad kyi don gyi phyir ro// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa chos rnam pa sna tshogs bstan pa dang rjes
34a8(rgyud): su 'thun zhing sngags kyi spod pa dang rje su 'thun pa legs par bstan pa nyid do// rgyal po chen po gang la la zhig 'das pa'i le'u 'di klog par 'gyur ba dang / 'dzin par
34b1(rgyud): 'gyur ba dang / yid la byed par 'gyur ba dang / g.yul gyi thog mar glang po che'i steng du bzhag pa dang / me tog dang / bdug pa dang / dri dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa rnam pa sna
34b2(rgyud): tshogs kyis mchod par byed na/ de la bdag cag byin gyis rlob par byed cing / phyir rgol ba dang / dgra bo dag kyang dbang du 'gyur la/ gzhan gyi dmags kyi dpung yang
34b3(rgyud): bshig par bgyi'o// glegs bam la bri ba byas te/ rang gi khyim du bzhag no/ de la rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo 'am/ rgyal po 'am/ rgyal po'i blon po 'am/
34b4(rgyud): rgyal mo 'am/ rgyal mo chen mo 'am/ dge slong ngam/ dge slong ma 'am/ dge bsnyen nam/ dge bsnyen ma dag la bsrang ba chen po dang / longs spyod chen po dang ldan pa
34b5(rgyud): dang / tshe ring ba nyid dang / tshe ba dang / nad med pa nyid dang / longs spyod rtag tu mngon par 'phel ba nyid kyang bgyi'o// de skad ces smras pa dang / thams cad dang ldan
34b6(rgyud): pa'i 'khor cang mi smra bar gyur to// // theg pa chen po sngags kyi spyod pa bstan pa'i cho ga zhib mo las byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa'i
34b7(rgyud): rnam par 'phral ba'i le'u rab 'byam rtsa ba'i cho ga zhib mo las 'dus pa'i le'u ste// dang po'o// /
34b8(rgyud): de nas 'jam dpal gzhan nur gyur pa thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor la bltas nas/ sems can thams cad kyi dam tshig la rjes su 'jug cing kun tu blta
35a1(rgyud): ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs so// 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa snyoms par bzhugs ma thag tu/ lte ba'i dkyil 'khor
35a2(rgyud): gyi phyogs nas/ 'od zer bye ba brgya stong du ma'i 'khor dang ldan pa'i 'od zer byung ste/ sems can gyi khams thams cad kun tu snang bar byas nas/ slar log ste gnas
35a3(rgyud): gtsang ma'i gzhal med khang snang bar byas nas 'khod par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la smras
35a4(rgyud): pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dam tshig la rjes su zhugs pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi le'u rab 'byam gyi spyod pa sgrub pa sems can thams cad kyi 'thun mong du gyur
35a5(rgyud): pa/ khyod kyi sngags kyi tshig gang du sems can yang dag par zhugs nas/ 'jig rten dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa thams cad kyi sngags grub pa yang dag par thob par
35a6(rgyud): 'gyur bas/ sems pa chen po khyod smros shig/ de skad ces smras pa dang / gsang ba'i bdag po gnod sbyin gyi bdag po la/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas mchog
35a7(rgyud): tu gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi rgyud smras pa/ rigs pa thams cad bskal pa zhes bya ba'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa ston par byed do// lag pa g.yas pa
35a8(rgyud): bteg nas/ sor mo'i rtse mo'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor la ston par byed de/ sor me'i rtse mo de las rig pa'i rgyal po bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma byung ste/
35b1(rgyud): byung nas kyang gnas gtsang ma'i gnas kyi gzhal med khang thams cad snang ba chen pos gnas par gyur to// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas/ khro bo'i rgyal/
35b2(rgyud): po gshin rje gshed kyi snying po las thams cad byed pa/ dpa' bo gcig pa spyan drangs pa dang / gshegs su gsol ba dang / zhi ba dang / rgyas pa dang / mngon spyod
35b3(rgyud): dang / mi snang ba dang / na mkha' la 'gro ba dang / sa 'og tu 'jug pa dang / chu la mi nub par 'gro ba dang / 'gug pa dang / rnam par dbye ba dang / dbang de byed
35b4(rgyud): pa dang / dri thams cad dang / phreng ba dang / mar me dag kyang rang gi rgyud kyi smin par byed de/ mdor na ji lta ji ltar sbyar ba de lta de ltar sgrub par byed pa ni yi ge gsum
35b5(rgyud): zhes bya ba ston pa sa chen po// don thams cad sgrub par byed pa/ khro bo'i rgyal po chen po'i sngags smras pa/ de dag gang zhe na/ oM A hUM/ 'di ni khro bo chen po'i
35b6(rgyud): snying po ste/ las byed pa dkyil 'khor thams cad dang / sngags thams cad kyi spyod pa sems pa chen po 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis smras te/ bgegs
35b7(rgyud): thams cad 'jig par byed pa'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa so// lag pa g.yas pa btegs pa ste/ khro bo'i spyi bor
35b8(rgyud): bzhag pa byas so// 'di skad du yang smras te/ sangs rgyas thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas bcom
36a1(rgyud): / ldan 'das rnams dgongs su gsol/ gang su dag phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams na rnam par gnas shing / mtha' yas mu med pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa'i
36a2(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' rnams dam tshig la lhag par gnas par gyis shig/ de skad ces smras nas/ khro ba'i rgyal po lag pa bskor nas btang bar gyur to// khro bo'i rgyal po chen po btang
36a3(rgyud): ma thag tu thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams dag tu song nas/ ska cig tsam gyi gang dag sdang ba'i bsam pa dang ldan pa'i sems can rdzu 'phrul che ba dag tshar bcad cing der bkug
36a4(rgyud): par gyur nas/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor chen po gnas gtsang ma'i gzhal med khang der rab tu bcug ste/ gnas ji lta ba bzhin du gnas par byas nas/ sems can ma rung ba dag
36a5(rgyud): la yang kan nas 'bar ba'i phreng ba'i tshog su byas shing / spyi bo la yang dag par gnas par byaso// de nas 'jam gzhon nur gyur pas/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de la yang
36a6(rgyud): ltas nas/ sems can khyed cag thams cad nyon cig/ gang yang dam tshig 'di las 'da' bar gyur na/ de la khro bo'i rgyal po 'dis chad pa dpyod par 'gyur te/ gang gi phyir na/
36a7(rgyud): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi dam tshig ni 'da' bar bya ba ma yin te/ sngags kyi don gyi tshig gsang ba byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul chen po dang ldan pa rnams kyi mdor
36a8(rgyud): brtan pa brjod par bya yis/ de legs par rab tu nyon la yid la bzung shig dang / bshad par bya'o//
36b1(rgyud): na ma sarba bud+ha nam/ oM ra ra sma ra/ a rba tita tA gas na/ ku ma rUb d+hA/ ri rdza d+ha d+ha baH swAhA/ grogs po dag 'dinga'i rtsa ba'i sngags yin te/ 'phags pa 'jam da/

36b8(rgyud): mthong ba bzhin du nye bar gnas pa/ byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa nyid bzhin du nye bar gnas pa/ sems can thams cad kyi don gyi phyir mchog
37a1(rgyud): tu gsang ba'i ngo bos nye bar gnas pa/ re ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa/ gang du dran pa tsam gyi mtshams med pa lnga yang yongs su sbyong

37a3(rgyud): snying po bdag nyid yin te/ sangs rgyas nyid bzhin du rab tu nye bar gnas pa yin no// mdor na bya ba thams cad la/ yon tan mtha' chen po brjod par ni bskal pa bye ba khrag

38b4(rgyud): sems can kan gyi mthong ba'o// na ma sa man+ta/ bud+ha nam/ a pra ti ha ta/ sha sa na nA ma/ tad+ya thA/ dza la dza la/ dz+wa la ya dza la ya/ hUM bi b+ho dau/ ka ha ri/ kri Sh+Ta/ sing+ga la swAH/

43b1(rgyud): bstan te// gdengs can dug ni gzhom bya'i phyir// 'dab chags tshul gyi rnam par rgyu// 'jig rten sngags ni ji srid pa// cho ga 'di ni brtan pa na// sems can gdul

99b3(rgyud): 'tsho chen las byang chu bo las/ byang chub srog chags skyon med pa'i// bzang pos khrus ni rab tu bya// sa dang lci ba'i phyi ma yis// sngags shes pas ni lus dril bya/ sngags
99b4(rgyud): kyi de bzhin dge byas pa'i// dri med gtsang sbrar byas po'i chus// sngags ldan bdag nyid khrus bya zhing // ha cang ring bar 'dug mi bya// de nas langs la chu ngogs 'dug/

319a3(rgyud): de bzhin rgyal ba'i mchod rten dang / sa rnam dag ni thams cad la// thams cad mdzes par byas par gyur// de tshe sngon gyi rgyal po des// bram ze de bzhin shag rigs skyes kang rgyal/
319a4(rgyud): shes rab ldan zhing no// byang chub mthar byed nga rgyal blo// de tshe dus kyi tha ma la// de nyid 'di'i grogs nyid 'gyur// rgyal po chos la dga' ba yis// rgyal rigs kyi ni mchog tu
319a5(rgyud): gsungs// lo ni nyi shu ba dan dang brgyad// de ni de tshe 'tsho bar 'gyur// bud med byas pa'i skyon nyid kyis// des byas nas ni lhag nas 'gro// blo ldan de ni mthar gyis kyang // bla med byang chub

319b1(rgyud): chos bdag nyid// dus byas nas ni lha gnas 'gro// lha rnams kyis ni rgyal thabs kyang // de bzhin mthar gyi byed par 'gyur// de nas de zhig nas kyang // mtho ris pas kyang mtho
319b2(rgyud): ris 'gro// de'i byang chub rgyud dang ni// dge ba'i chos ni yongs rdzogs byas// de'i ngan nyid rgyal po ste// rgyal srid gnod med byed par 'gyur// yi ge'i dang po ya zhes bya// sa'i dang po lung

319b7(rgyud): bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad du// de tshes la rgyal srid byas// bram ze rnams la nor byin nas// the tshom med par dus kyang byas// de nas gzhan yang sa bdag gi// de tshe rgyal po bzang po byung
